 Smartphone hacking is common, but now the era of Smart TV hacking is
 bharat main Smart TV kaa trend shuru ho chukaa he or ab log tradishnal tivi ke bajaae Smart TV ko tarjeeh de rahe hai
 Since Smart TV works on roughly the same type of software as your smartphone
 Smart TV ke liye aapako internet kii bhi jarurat hoti he
 So Smart TV hacking is getting easier now and hackers are targeting it
 samsung TV market main bhi kaaphi aage he or haal hi main company ne apni oficial website par Smart TV ko hekking or khatarnaak code se bachaane ke tareeke bataae hai
 Now some such smart tvs will be available in the market which have built in microphones
 microphone dene kaa makasad ise wais cmand ke jariye chalaanaa he
 Currently there are such TV trends where voice commands can be given from remote
 kuch Smart TV aise bhi hai jinamein Always On wais cmand kaa system he
 In such a situation, it is not at all difficult for the hackers to listen to your conversation through the TV in your bedroom
 smart tivi main kai eps hote hai, smart tivi ke liye dedicated ap store hote hai jahaan se yugers alag alag ap downlod karte hai
 There are also Smart tvs in the market which also have a camera
 ab aap is baat kaa khud andaja laga len ki koi haikar aapaki smart tivi hack karke camera or microphone ko control kar le
 There is a TV in front of you in the bedroom and you do not even know who is watching you and listening to you
 bhaskar kii ek report ke mutabikbharat main hi aisi ghatnaayen saamne ai hai jahaan smart tivi ko hack karke ek kapal kaa video viral kar diya gaya or duusare maamle main blakemeling bhi kii gai
 The day you hear the news that apps containing malware were found in the Google Play Store, which hacked users' mobile phones
 isi tarah Smart TV ke liye die gaye ap store main bhi mailaware vaale install kiye ja sakate hai or yugers inke jhaanse main aasaani se aa sakate hai
 Companies understand your watch history through Smart TV and give content and advertisements accordingly, this is not a new thing
 kuch saal pehle 2013 main Black Hat conference ke dauraan kai Smart TV modells kii hekking kaa demonstrishan kiya gaya
 During this, it was shown that hackers can take control of social apps of Smart TV
 itnaa hi nahin, files acces karke unhen modiphai bhi kiya ja saktaa he
 This is the solution to every problem, save smart TV from being hacked
 pareshaan hone kii jarurat nahin he, kyonki technolji ko sef yuj karnaa hi samajhadaari he

 --- settings main ja kar microphone kii olves on opshan ko of kar den
 --- Do not ignore the updates given by the company and keep updating on time
 --- apane Smart TV main gaurajaruri eps install na karen, khaas kar jinke bare main aapako pataa nahin he
 --- Turn on Smart Security by going to the Accessibility section of the System Settings of Samsung's Smart TV
 --- third party remote ap yuj na karen, company kii taraf se diya gaya remote hi yuj karen
 --- Do not connect Smart TV to any open wifi
 sicyor conection kaa hi yuj karen

 sarkaar kii ye niti intlexul property ko bazaar main bikne laayak puunji or aarthik hathiyaar banane kii baat karata he
 At the same time, this policy encourages all Indian and foreign corporate companies to make more use of IPR law and increase the patent rule
 sarkaar kahati he ki is niti se nai-nai khojon or avishkaron ko badhaava milegaa, lekin dablutio par research kar rahe jaankaar isse sahamat nahin hai
 Professor Abhijit Das, head of the Center for WTO Studies at the Indian Institute of Foreign Trade in Delhi, says, "to date, nowhere has it been proven that stringent IPR laws encourage inventions and new discoveries
" isliye ye kahana ki nai khojon ke liye kade ipiar banaae ja rahe hai, main isse sahamat nahin hum
 ' nai niti ko sarkaar creative india, innovative india ke naare se jod rahi he, lekin is niti ke peeche america bahurashtriya companiyon kaa dabaav dikhataa he jo dawaaon se lekar krishi or shiksha ke kshetra main patent raaj ko badhanaa chaahati hai
